xml:space="preserve">3  X 10 Tablets Metclass G1 & G2 – Short Description Metclass G1 and Metclass G2 are oral antidiabetic tablets formulated to help achieve effective glycemic control in adults with  Type 2 diabetes mellitus . They combine  Glimepiride  with  Metformin Hydrochloride  to provide dual-action blood glucose management by enhancing insulin release and reducing hepatic glucose production while improving insulin sensitivity. These formulations help control both fasting and postprandial blood sugar levels, support long-term HbA1c reduction, and may lower the risk of diabetes-related complications when used alongside a healthy diet and regular exercise. Metclass G1 and G2 should be taken only under the guidance of a qualified healthcare professional. 33)IMUCLAV DUO/ULTRA Dry Syrup :- <w:tblPr><w:tblStyle w:val="TableGrid"/><w:tblpPr Description  IMUCLAV-1000  is a broad-spectrum antibiotic tablet containing  Amoxicillin 875 mg  and  Potassium Clavulanate 125 mg , formulated to treat a wide range of bacterial infections. This combination effectively kills susceptible bacteria while clavulanic acid inhibits beta-lactamase enzymes, helping overcome bacterial resistance and enhancing the antibiotic's effectiveness. IMUCLAV-1000 is commonly prescribed for respiratory tract infections, ear, nose and throat infections, urinary tract infections, skin and soft tissue infections, dental infections, and bone and joint infections. It helps provide rapid symptom relief and promotes faster recovery when taken as prescribed. IMUCLAV-1000 should be used only under the supervision of a qualified healthcare professional.
